AOL Macro Fonts (fixed)
These fonts have been adjusted to render correctly on modern OSes. Older versions of Windows rendered Arial differently (some characters had different widths than today and the text encoding was Windows-1251 instead of unicode). I hope to fix all of the fonts, but it'll probably take a while. Side note: These text art fonts use the font of Arial, they are non-monospaced.
